Users can mark code sections with `#region` and `#endregion` comments (with optional names), and navigate between them using a quick-pick command menu.\n\n## Implementation Overview\n\n### Core Components\n\n#### 1. **NamedRegionRangeProvider** (`namedRegionProvider.ts`)\n- Implements `RangeProvider` interface for the VS Code folding system\n- Scans text model for `#region` and `#endregion` markers\n- Extracts region names from markers\n- Returns `FoldingRegions` object for integration with folding subsystem\n- Supports nested regions with proper stack-based tracking\n\n#### 2. **Region Detection Functions** (`namedRegionProvider.ts`)\n- `extractNamedRegions()` - Returns array of NamedRegion objects\n- `computeNamedRegionRanges()` - Returns FoldingRegions for folding subsystem\n- `extractRegionName()` - Parses region name from comment line\n- `isEndregionMarker()` - Detects end-of-region markers\n\n#### 3. **GoToNamedRegionAction** (`goToNamedRegionAction.ts` / in `folding.ts`)\n- EditorAction that provides the \"Go to Named Region\" command\n- Binds to `Ctrl+Shift+R` / `Cmd+Shift+R`\n- Shows quick-pick menu of all regions in current file\n- Navigates to selected region with auto-unfolding\n- Displays region names and starting line numbers in UI\n\n#### 4. **Test Suite** (`namedRegionProvider.test.ts`)\n- Comprehensive tests for region detection\n- Covers simple, multiple, and nested regions\n- Tests various comment styles\n- Validates edge cases and error handling\n\n## File Structure\n\n```\nsrc/vs/editor/contrib/folding/\n├── browser/\n│   ├── namedRegionProvider.ts          ← Core provider implementation\n│   ├── goToNamedRegionAction.ts        ← Navigation action (standalone)\n│   └── folding.ts                      ← Modified to integrate GoToNamedRegionAction\n└── test/browser/\n    └── namedRegionProvider.test.ts     ← Test suite\n```\n\n## Key Features\n\n✅ **Marker Detection**\n- Detects `#region <name>` and `#endregion` markers\n- Case-insensitive matching\n- Supports various comment styles:\n  - `//` (JavaScript, TypeScript, Go, etc.)\n  - `/* */` (C-style languages)\n  - `#` (Python, Bash, etc.)\n  - `--` (SQL, Lua, etc.)\n  - `<!--` (HTML/XML)\n\n✅ **Region Management**\n- Extracts custom names from markers\n- Supports nested regions\n- Proper stack-based tracking of region nesting\n- Handles unmatched or unclosed regions gracefully\n\n✅ **Navigation**\n- Quick-pick menu for region selection\n- Shows region names and line numbers\n- Auto-centers view on selected region\n- Automatically unfolds collapsed regions\n\n✅ **Integration**\n- Implements standard `RangeProvider` interface\n- Provides `namedRegion:<name>` type marking\n- Respects folding limits from configuration\n- Integrates seamlessly with existing folding system\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Region Marking\n\n```typescript\n// #region Utilities\nfunction helper1() { }\nfunction helper2() { }\n// #endregion\n\n// #region Main Logic\nfunction main() {\n    // implementation\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Multi-line Comments\n\n```python\n# #region Data Processing\ndef load_data():\n    pass\n\ndef transform_data():\n    pass\n# #endregion\n```\n\n### Block Comments\n\n```c\n/* #region Error Handling */\nvoid handle_error(int code) {\n    // error handling logic\n}\n/* #endregion */\n```\n\n### Nested Regions\n\n```typescript\n// #region Module\nnamespace Module {\n    // #region Public API\n    export function publicFunction() { }\n    // #endregion\n\n    // #region Internals\n    function internalHelper() { }\n    // #endregion\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n## Navigation\n\n1. **Open Region Picker:** Press `Ctrl+Shift+R` (Windows/Linux) or `Cmd+Shift+R` (macOS)\n2. **Select Region:** Type to filter or use arrow keys to navigate\n3. **Go To Region:** Press Enter or click region\n4. **Auto Unfold:** The region will automatically unfold if collapsed\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Region Name Extraction\n\nThe implementation uses a regex pattern to extract region names from various comment formats:\n\n```\n#region\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s*(?:-->|$|\\*/))?$\n```\n\nThis pattern:\n- Matches `#region` (case-insensitive)\n- Captures the name (group 1)\n- Handles trailing delimiters (`-->`, `*/`)\n- Trims whitespace from extracted names\n\n### Stack-Based Region Tracking\n\nRegions are tracked using a stack structure:\n- When `#region` is found, push to stack\n- When `#endregion` is found, pop from stack and create range\n- Last pushed region is matched with next popped `#endregion`\n- Supports arbitrary nesting depth\n\n### FoldingRegions Integration\n\nNamed regions are integrated into VS Code's folding system:\n- Each region becomes a foldable range\n- Region type is marked as `namedRegion:<name>`\n- Respects editor folding limits\n- Works with existing fold/unfold operations\n\n## Testing\n\n### Test Coverage\n\nThe test suite verifies:\n\n1. **Basic Users can mark code sections with `#region` and `#endregion` comments (with optional names), and navigate between them using a quick-pick command menu.\n\n## Implementation Overview\n\n### Core Components\n\n#### 1. **NamedRegionRangeProvider** (`namedRegionProvider.ts`)\n- Implements `RangeProvider` interface for the VS Code folding system\n- Scans text model for `#region` and `#endregion` markers\n- Extracts region names from markers\n- Returns `FoldingRegions` object for integration with folding subsystem\n- Supports nested regions with proper stack-based tracking\n\n#### 2. **Region Detection Functions** (`namedRegionProvider.ts`)\n- `extractNamedRegions()` - Returns array of NamedRegion objects\n- `computeNamedRegionRanges()` - Returns FoldingRegions for folding subsystem\n- `extractRegionName()` - Parses region name from comment line\n- `isEndregionMarker()` - Detects end-of-region markers\n\n#### 3. **GoToNamedRegionAction** (`goToNamedRegionAction.ts` / in `folding.ts`)\n- EditorAction that provides the \"Go to Named Region\" command\n- Binds to `Ctrl+Shift+R` / `Cmd+Shift+R`\n- Shows quick-pick menu of all regions in current file\n- Navigates to selected region with auto-unfolding\n- Displays region names and starting line numbers in UI\n\n#### 4. **Test Suite** (`namedRegionProvider.test.ts`)\n- Comprehensive tests for region detection\n- Covers simple, multiple, and nested regions\n- Tests various comment styles\n- Validates edge cases and error handling\n\n## File Structure\n\n```\nsrc/vs/editor/contrib/folding/\n├── browser/\n│   ├── namedRegionProvider.ts          ← Core provider implementation\n│   ├── goToNamedRegionAction.ts        ← Navigation action (standalone)\n│   └── folding.ts                      ← Modified to integrate GoToNamedRegionAction\n└── test/browser/\n    └── namedRegionProvider.test.ts     ← Test suite\n```\n\n## Key Features\n\n✅ **Marker Detection**\n- Detects `#region <name>` and `#endregion` markers\n- Case-insensitive matching\n- Supports various comment styles:\n  - `//` (JavaScript, TypeScript, Go, etc.)\n  - `/* */` (C-style languages)\n  - `#` (Python, Bash, etc.)\n  - `--` (SQL, Lua, etc.)\n  - `<!--` (HTML/XML)\n\n✅ **Region Management**\n- Extracts custom names from markers\n- Supports nested regions\n- Proper stack-based tracking of region nesting\n- Handles unmatched or unclosed regions gracefully\n\n✅ **Navigation**\n- Quick-pick menu for region selection\n- Shows region names and line numbers\n- Auto-centers view on selected region\n- Automatically unfolds collapsed regions\n\n✅ **Integration**\n- Implements standard `RangeProvider` interface\n- Provides `namedRegion:<name>` type marking\n- Respects folding limits from configuration\n- Integrates seamlessly with existing folding system\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Region Marking\n\n```typescript\n// #region Utilities\nfunction helper1() { }\nfunction helper2() { }\n// #endregion\n\n// #region Main Logic\nfunction main() {\n    // implementation\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Multi-line Comments\n\n```python\n# #region Data Processing\ndef load_data():\n    pass\n\ndef transform_data():\n    pass\n# #endregion\n```\n\n### Block Comments\n\n```c\n/* #region Error Handling */\nvoid handle_error(int code) {\n    // error handling logic\n}\n/* #endregion */\n```\n\n### Nested Regions\n\n```typescript\n// #region Module\nnamespace Module {\n    // #region Public API\n    export function publicFunction() { }\n    // #endregion\n\n    // #region Internals\n    function internalHelper() { }\n    // #endregion\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n## Navigation\n\n1. **Open Region Picker:** Press `Ctrl+Shift+R` (Windows/Linux) or `Cmd+Shift+R` (macOS)\n2. **Select Region:** Type to filter or use arrow keys to navigate\n3. **Go To Region:** Press Enter or click region\n4. **Auto Unfold:** The region will automatically unfold if collapsed\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Region Name Extraction\n\nThe implementation uses a regex pattern to extract region names from various comment formats:\n\n```\n#region\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s*(?:-->|$|\\*/))?$\n```\n\nThis pattern:\n- Matches `#region` (case-insensitive)\n- Captures the name (group 1)\n- Handles trailing delimiters (`-->`, `*/`)\n- Trims whitespace from extracted names\n\n### Stack-Based Region Tracking\n\nRegions are tracked using a stack structure:\n- When `#region` is found, push to stack\n- When `#endregion` is found, pop from stack and create range\n- Last pushed region is matched with next popped `#endregion`\n- Supports arbitrary nesting depth\n\n### FoldingRegions Integration\n\nNamed regions are integrated into VS Code's folding system:\n- Each region becomes a foldable range\n- Region type is marked as `namedRegion:<name>`\n- Respects editor folding limits\n- Works with existing fold/unfold operations\n\n## Testing\n\n### Test Coverage\n\nThe test suite verifies:\n\n1. **Basic Detection**\n   - Simple region extraction\n   - Region name parsing\n   - Line number tracking\n\n2. **Complex Scenarios**\n   - Multiple regions in one file\n   - Nested region support\n   - Various comment styles\n\n3. **Edge Cases**\n   - Unmatched endregion markers\n   - Unclosed regions\n   - Whitespace handling\n   - Case sensitivity\n\n4. **Integration**\n   - FoldingRegions computation\n   - Proper type assignment\n   - Limit enforcement\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\n# Run all named region tests\nnpm test -- namedRegionProvider\n\n# Run specific test\nnpm test -- \"Extract simple named region\"\n\n# Run with verbose output\nnpm test -- --verbose namedRegionProvider\n```\n\n## Integration with folding.ts\n\nTo fully integrate this feature, add to `folding.ts`:\n\n1. **Import statements** (after existing imports):\n```typescript\nimport { IQuickInputService } from '../../../../platform/quickinput/common/quickInput.js';\nimport { extractNamedRegions } from './namedRegionProvider.js';\n```\n\n2. **GoToNamedRegionAction class** (see goToNamedRegionAction.ts)\n\n3. **Action registration** (with other action registrations):\n```typescript\nregisterEditorAction(GoToNamedRegionAction);\n```\n\nSee `INTEGRATION_GUIDE.md` for detailed integration instructions.\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Design Principles\n\n1. **Separation of Concerns**\n   - Provider handles region detection\n   - Action handles user interaction\n   - Tests validate both\n\n2. **Extensibility**\n   - Implements standard `RangeProvider` interface\n   - Can be combined with other providers\n   - Region type marking allows future enhancements\n\n3. **Robustness**\n   - Graceful handling of malformed markers\n   - Support for various comment styles\n   - Comprehensive error handling\n\n4. **Performance**\n   - Single-pass line scanning\n   - Linear time complexity\n   - Minimal memory overhead\n\n## Limitations\n\n- Region markers must be exact (case-insensitive `#region`/`#endregion`)\n- Names are extracted from the comment content, not from separate metadata\n- No support for region hierarchies beyond nesting (e.g., no category tags)\n- Region markers consume a full line (good practice, but required)\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements:\n\n1. **Visual Enhancements**\n   - Region name display in gutter\n   - Region breadcrumb in editor\n   - Syntax highlighting for markers\n   - Custom colors per region type\n\n2. **Advanced Navigation**\n   - Region outline panel\n   - Go to next/previous region commands\n   - Region selection highlighting\n   - Region folding profiles\n\n3. **Configuration**\n   - Custom region marker patterns\n   - Region-specific indentation\n   - Auto-fold by default\n   - Region type categories\n\n4. **Integration**\n   - Outline view integration\n   - Breadcrumb navigation\n   - Region-aware refactoring\n   - Code folding templates\n\n## License\n\nThis implementation follows the same license as VS Code (MIT License). super({\n            id: 'editor.action.goToNamedRegion',\n            label: nls.localize2('goToNamedRegion.label', \"Go to Named Region\"),\n            precondition: CONTEXT_FOLDING_ENABLED,\n            kbOpts: {\n                kbExpr: EditorContextKeys.editorTextFocus,\n                primary: KeyChord(KeyMod.CtrlCmd | KeyMod.Shift | KeyCode.KeyR),\n                weight: KeybindingWeight.EditorContrib\n            }\n        });\n    }\n    async run(accessor: ServicesAccessor, editor: ICodeEditor): Promise<void> {\n        const quickInputService = accessor.get(IQuickInputService);\n        const model = editor.getModel();\n        if (!model) return;\n        const regions = extractNamedRegions(model);\n        if (regions.length === 0) {\n            quickInputService.showInputBox({\n                placeHolder: nls.localize('noNamedRegions', 'No named regions found')\n            });\n            return;\n        }\n        const items = regions.map((region) => ({\n            label: region.name,\n            description: `Line ${region.startLineNumber}`,\n            region: region\n        }));\n        const selected = await quickInputService.pick(items, {\n            placeHolder: nls.localize('selectNamedRegion', 'Select a region'),\n            matchOnDescription: true\n        });\n        if (!selected) return;\n        const region = selected.region;\n        editor.setSelection({\n            startLineNumber: region.startLineNumber,\n            startColumn: 1,\n            endLineNumber: region.startLineNumber,\n            endColumn: 1\n        });\n        editor.revealLineInCenter(region.startLineNumber, ScrollType.Smooth);\n        const foldingController = FoldingController.get(editor);\n        if (foldingController) {\n            const foldingModelPromise = foldingController.getFoldingModel();\n            if (foldingModelPromise) {\n                foldingModelPromise.then(foldingModel => {\n                    if (foldingModel) {\n                        const regions = foldingModel.regions;\n                        for (let i = 0; i < regions.length; i++) {\n                            if (regions.getStartLineNumber(i) === region.startLineNumber &&\n                                regions.getEndLineNumber(i) === region.endLineNumber) {\n                                if (regions.isCollapsed(i)) {\n                                    regions.setCollapsed(i, false);\n                                    foldingController.triggerFoldingModelChanged();\n                                }\n                                break;\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                });\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Change 3:** Add registration after line 1263\n```typescript\nregisterEditorAction(GoToNamedRegionAction);\n```\n\n### 3.
